 Page 1 - 127LR2081(01) -1 
 Emergency preamble. Whereas, acts and resolves of the Legislature do not 1 
become effective until 90 days after adjournment unless enacted as emergencies; and  2 
Whereas, the 90 -day period will not terminate until after the beginning of the next 3 
fiscal year; an d 4 
Whereas, certain obligations and expenses incident to the operation of state 5 
departments and institutions will become due and payable immediately; and  6 
Whereas, in the judgment of the Legislature, these facts create an emergency within 7 
the meaning of the Constitution of Maine and require the following legislation as 8 
immediately necessary for the preservation of the public peace, health and safety; now, 9 
therefore,  10 
Be it enacted by the People of the State of Maine as follows:  11 
PART A  12

allocations are made.  14

Sec. D -1.  36 MRSA §1811, first ¶, as repealed and replaced by PL 2013, c . 588, 11 
Pt. E, §11, is amended to read:  12 
A tax is imposed on the value of all tangible personal property, products transferred 13 
electronically and taxable services sold at retail in this State.  The rate of tax is 7% on the 14 
value of liquor sold in licensed es tablishments as defined in Title 28 -A, section 2, 15 
subsection 15, in accordance with Title 28 -A, chapter 43; 7% on the value of rental of 16 
living quarters in any hotel, rooming house or tourist or trailer camp; 10% on the value of 17 
rental for a period of less  than one year of an automobile, of a pickup truck or van with a 18 
gross vehicle weight of less than 26,000 pounds rented from a person primarily engaged 19 
in the business of renting automobiles or of a loaner vehicle that is provided other than to 20 
a motor veh icle dealer's service customers pursuant to a manufacturer’s or dealer’s 21 
warranty; 7% on the value of prepared food; and 5% on the value of all other tangible 22 
personal property and taxable services and products transferred electronically.  23 
Notwithstanding the other provisions of this section, from October 1, 2013 to June 30  24 
July 31 , 2015, the rate of tax is 8% on the value of rental of living quarters in any hotel, 25 
rooming house or tourist or trailer camp; 8% on the value of prepared food; 8% on the 26 
value o f liquor sold in licensed establishments as defined in Title 28 -A, section 2, 27 
subsection 15, in accordance with Title 28 -A, chapter 43; and 5.5% on the value of all 28 
other tangible personal property and taxable services and products transferred 29 
electronical ly.  Value is measured by the sale price, except as otherwise provided. The 30 
value of rental for a period of less than one year of an automobile or of a pickup truck or 31 
van with a gross vehicle weight of less than 26,000 pounds rented from a person 32 
primaril y engaged in the business of renting automobiles is the total rental charged to the 33 
lessee and includes, but is not limited to, maintenance and service contracts, drop -off or 34 
pick-up fees, airport surcharges, mileage fees and any separately itemized charge s on the 35 
rental agreement to recover the owner’s estimated costs of the charges imposed by 36 
government authority for title fees, inspection fees, local excise tax and agent fees on all 37 
vehicles in its rental fleet registered in the State.  All fees must be disclosed when an 38 
estimated quote is provided to the lessee.  39

9.  Fiscal  Stability Program.   The Fiscal Stability Program is established to ensure 22

SUMMARY  5 
PART A  6 
This Part makes appropriations and allocations through July 31, 2015.  7 
PART B  8 
This Part reduces the percentage of tax revenue transferred to the Local Government 9 
Fund for th e purpose of state -municipal revenue sharing from 5% to 2%.  10 
PART C  11 
This Part establishes the state contribution to the total cost of funding public 12 
education from kindergarten to grade 12 for the month of July 2015.  13 
PART D  14 
This Part extends by one month th e current sales and use tax rates to July 31, 2015.  15 
PART E  16 
This Part continues authorization for each individual tax expenditure provided by 17 
statute.  18 
PART F  19 
This Part gives the Department of Health and Human Services the authority to adopt 20 
emergency rules to implement any provisions of this legislation over which the 21 
department has specific authority that has not been addressed by some other Part without 22 
the necessity of demonstrating that immediate adoption is necessary to avoid a threat to 23 
public health, safety or welfare.  24 
PART G  25 
This Part authorizes the Department of Health and Human Services to transfer 26 
available balances of appropriations between the MaineCare General Fund accounts for 27 
the month of July 2015.  28 
PART H  29 
This Part amends the Fiscal Stability  Program in the Department of Inland Fisheries 30 
and Wildlife to delay the additional appropriation until the 2018 -2019 biennium.  31 
PART I  32 
 
 Page 175 - 127LR2081(01) -1 
 This Part continues limited -period positions set to expire during June 2015 through 1 
July 31, 2015.  2 
PART J  3 
This Part provi des that the purpose of this legislation is to provide for the obligations 4 
of the State necessary for the operation of state departments through July 31, 2015.  This 5 
Part also provides for the repeal of this legislation on the date the 2016 -2017 biennial 6 
budget becomes law.  7
